Notice
No Legal responsibility is accepted for the publication of advertisements regarding 
change of name in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette. Persons notifying the changes 
will remain solely responsible for the legal consequences and also for any other 
misrepresentation, etc.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE 	
 [Part VI—Sec. 4
Public  NoticeS
P. Vadivelan, a Male child born to Thiru N. Paraman on 25th November 1988, residing at  No. 46, Veeramudaiyan 
2nd Street, Muthupatti, Pazhanganatham Post, Madurai-625 003, after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery she has been 
living  as a female (reference Dr. P. Raja, MS, Mch (uro), Professor head dept of Urology, Government Rajaji Hospital, 
Madurai-625 020. By this I, Could be treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as P. BHAVANA.
Madurai,		
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
P.VADIVELAN	
 
9th March 2020.
Sinil P.S., a Male child born to Thiru P.U Sasikumar, on 16th January 1983, residing at No. 132, West Namchivayapuram, 
Choolaimedu, Chennai-600 094. Has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery done by 
Dr. Vishnu, MBBS, MS, Mch, DNB MNAMSc, Plastic Surgeon (Reg No: 24700) at Rajeev Gandhi Government Medical College. 
By This I, May be Treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as SANJANA S
Chennai,	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
         SINIL P.S. 
13th  March  2020.
